line-height:1.2" class="fltlft ">					<span style="font-size:9px; color:#660000; text-shadow:1px 1px 1px #FFF;">Monday, October  1 2012, 06:42 AM EDT</span>				</div>        				<div style="float:left; width:605px;"> 					<span class="h2story">Looking to raise awareness at ArtPrize </span>					<div style="border-left:1px solid #CCC; margin-left:5px; padding-left:5px; padding-top:5px"><br><p style="margin-bottom: 0in"><font color="#000000"><font face="Arial, sans-serif"><font style="font-size: 13pt" size="3">GRAND<br>RAPIDS, Mich. (NEWSCHANNEL 3) – ArtPrize is in full swing in Grand<br>Rapids, and the event is being used to raise awareness not only of<br>art, but also about sex trafficking. </font></font></font><br></p><br><p style="margin-bottom: 0in"><br><br></p><br><p style="margin-bottom: 0in"><font color="#000000"><font face="Arial, sans-serif"><font style="font-size: 13pt" size="3">A<br>Grand Rapids group is hoping that a 'milk' carton giveaway at<br>ArtPrize will draw attention to the cause of human sex trafficking<br>and child homelessness. They hope that giving away cartons containing<br>water will help make people more aware of the problem in West<br>Michigan. </font></font></font><br></p><br><p style="margin-bottom: 0in"><br><br></p><br><p style="margin-bottom: 0in"><font color="#000000"><font face="Arial, sans-serif"><font style="font-size: 13pt" size="3">More<br>than 6,000 cartons of water will be given out along the blue bridge<br>in Grand Rapids over the weekend, all of them asking the same<br>question, 'Have you seen me?' tying into 'The Child' exhibit which<br>showcases a sexual assault victim from West Michigan. </font></font></font><br></p><br><p style="margin-bottom: 0in"><br><br></p><br><p style="margin-bottom: 0in"><font color="#000000">“<font face="Arial, sans-serif"><font style="font-size: 13pt" size="3">No<br>one wakes up one morning and says 'I am going to sell myself today or<br>be sold,'” said Andy Soper of the Manasseh Project. </font></font></font><br></p><br><p style="margin-bottom: 0in"><br><br></p><br><p style="margin-bottom: 0in"><font color="#000000"><font face="Arial, sans-serif"><font style="font-size: 13pt" size="3">The<br>Manesseh Project says that many homeless kids are sexually exploited<br>and are working to raise awareness of the warning signs of<br>trafficking. </font></font></font><br></p><br><p style="margin-bottom: what they have to do to<br>survive on the streets,” said Soper. </font></font></font><br></p><br><p style="margin-bottom: 0in"><br><br></p><br><p style="margin-bottom: 0in"><font color="#000000"><font face="Arial, sans-serif"><font style="font-size: 13pt" size="3">Anywhere<br>from 1.6 to 2.8 million kids run away each year, but not enough of us<br>know why it is happening. </font></font></font><br></p><br><p style="margin-bottom: 0in"><br><br></p><br><p style="margin-bottom: 0in"><font color="#000000"><font face="Arial, sans-serif"><font style="font-size: 13pt"
